\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_source}{astcenc\+\_\+internal.\+h}} 파일의 \mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_source_l00068}{68}} 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_a2cce51c3362aa0b5040437ac0e7f8969}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!promise@{promise}}
\index{promise@{promise}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{promise}{promise}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a2cce51c3362aa0b5040437ac0e7f8969} 
\#define promise(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{cond}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})~assert(cond)}



Functions and data declarations. 

Make a promise to the compiler\textquotesingle{}s optimizer.

A promise is an expression that the optimizer is can assume is true for to help it generate faster code. Common use cases for this are to promise that a for loop will iterate more than once, or that the loop iteration count is a multiple of a vector length, which avoids pre-\/loop checks and can avoid loop tails if loops are unrolled by the auto-\/vectorizer. 

\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_source}{astcenc\+\_\+internal.\+h}} 파일의 \mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_source_l00061}{61}} 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a319cc507e110bedc1da79eeb325cb64c} 
template$<$typename T $>$ \\
T \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} aligned\+\_\+malloc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{size}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{align}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Allocate an aligned memory buffer. 

Allocated memory must be freed by aligned\+\_\+free.


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em size} & The desired buffer size. \\
\hline
{\em align} & The desired buffer alignment; must be 2\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}N, may be increased by the implementation to a minimum allowable alignment.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The memory buffer pointer or nullptr on allocation failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a579b9a2ceeecda2fb3abe63b8311df1c} 
void compress\+\_\+block (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__contexti}{astcenc\+\_\+contexti}} \&}]{ctx}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{pcb}{\mbox{[}16\mbox{]}, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structcompression__working__buffers}{compression\+\_\+working\+\_\+buffers}} \&}]{tmpbuf}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compress an image block into a physical block. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em ctx} & The compressor context and configuration. \\
\hline
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to compress. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em pcb} & The physical compressed block output. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em tmpbuf} & Preallocated scratch buffers for the compressor. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Compute the angular endpoints for one plane for each block mode.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a878f3a9f6a593b072db1abbf122081e3} 
void compute\+\_\+avgs\+\_\+and\+\_\+dirs\+\_\+2\+\_\+comp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__info}{partition\+\_\+info}} \&}]{pi}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{component1}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{component2}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__metrics}{partition\+\_\+metrics}}}]{pm}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONS\mbox{]}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute averages and dominant directions for each partition in a 2 component texture. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em pi} & The partition info for the current trial. \\
\hline
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to be compressed. \\
\hline
 & {\em component1} & The first component included in the analysis. \\
\hline
 & {\em component2} & The second component included in the analysis. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em pm} & The output partition metrics.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Only pi.\+partition\+\_\+count array entries actually get initialized.
\item Direction vectors {\ttfamily pm.\+dir} are not normalized. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

void compute\+\_\+avgs\+\_\+and\+\_\+dirs\+\_\+3\+\_\+comp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__info}{partition\+\_\+info}} \&}]{pi}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{omitted\+\_\+component}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__metrics}{partition\+\_\+metrics}}}]{pm}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONS\mbox{]}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute averages and dominant directions for each partition in a 3 component texture. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em pi} & The partition info for the current trial. \\
\hline
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to be compressed. \\
\hline
 & {\em omitted\+\_\+component} & The component excluded from the analysis. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em pm} & The output partition metrics.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Only pi.\+partition\+\_\+count array entries actually get initialized.
\item Direction vectors {\ttfamily pm.\+dir} are not normalized. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{compute\_avgs\_and\_dirs\_3\_comp\_rgb@{compute\_avgs\_and\_dirs\_3\_comp\_rgb}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{compute\_avgs\_and\_dirs\_3\_comp\_rgb()}{compute\_avgs\_and\_dirs\_3\_comp\_rgb()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a73936e5cf41b74f2b8d9b137a9d64253} 
void compute\+\_\+avgs\+\_\+and\+\_\+dirs\+\_\+3\+\_\+comp\+\_\+rgb (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__info}{partition\+\_\+info}} \&}]{pi}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__metrics}{partition\+\_\+metrics}}}]{pm}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONS\mbox{]}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute averages and dominant directions for each partition in a 3 component texture. 

This is a specialization of {\ttfamily compute\+\_\+avgs\+\_\+and\+\_\+dirs\+\_\+3\+\_\+comp} where the omitted component is always alpha, a common case during partition search.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em pi} & The partition info for the current trial. \\
\hline
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to be compressed. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em pm} & The output partition metrics.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Only pi.\+partition\+\_\+count array entries actually get initialized.
\item Direction vectors {\ttfamily pm.\+dir} are not normalized. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__averages__and__directions_8cpp_source}{astcenc\+\_\+averages\+\_\+and\+\_\+directions.\+cpp}} 파일의 \mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__averages__and__directions_8cpp_source_l00568}{568}} 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a00407861c2f0e767b64b1cb1bb7a27b6} 
void compute\+\_\+avgs\+\_\+and\+\_\+dirs\+\_\+4\+\_\+comp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__info}{partition\+\_\+info}} \&}]{pi}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__metrics}{partition\+\_\+metrics}}}]{pm}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONS\mbox{]}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute averages and dominant directions for each partition in a 4 component texture. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em pi} & The partition info for the current trial. \\
\hline
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to be compressed. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em pm} & The output partition metrics.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Only pi.\+partition\+\_\+count array entries actually get initialized.
\item Direction vectors {\ttfamily pm.\+dir} are not normalized. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_aa4077e6408620eefddd42b7e159dc93c}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!compute\_error\_of\_weight\_set\_1plane@{compute\_error\_of\_weight\_set\_1plane}}
\index{compute\_error\_of\_weight\_set\_1plane@{compute\_error\_of\_weight\_set\_1plane}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{compute\_error\_of\_weight\_set\_1plane()}{compute\_error\_of\_weight\_set\_1plane()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_aa4077e6408620eefddd42b7e159dc93c} 
float compute\+\_\+error\+\_\+of\+\_\+weight\+\_\+set\+\_\+1plane (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structendpoints__and__weights}{endpoints\+\_\+and\+\_\+weights}} \&}]{eai}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structdecimation__info}{decimation\+\_\+info}} \&}]{di}{, }\item[{const float \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+quant\+\_\+uvalue}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the error of a decimated weight set for 1 plane. 

After computing ideal weights for the case with one weight per texel, we want to compute the error for decimated weight grids where weights are stored at a lower resolution. This function computes the error of the reduced grid, compared to the full grid.


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em eai} & The ideal weights for the full grid. \\
\hline
{\em di} & The selected weight decimation. \\
\hline
{\em dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+quant\+\_\+uvalue} & The quantized weights for the decimated grid.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The accumulated error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{compute\_error\_of\_weight\_set\_2planes()}{compute\_error\_of\_weight\_set\_2planes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a09a63c4b1e684f7ff9d88e5717b10bfb} 
float compute\+\_\+error\+\_\+of\+\_\+weight\+\_\+set\+\_\+2planes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structendpoints__and__weights}{endpoints\+\_\+and\+\_\+weights}} \&}]{eai1}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structendpoints__and__weights}{endpoints\+\_\+and\+\_\+weights}} \&}]{eai2}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structdecimation__info}{decimation\+\_\+info}} \&}]{di}{, }\item[{const float \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+quant\+\_\+uvalue\+\_\+plane1}{, }\item[{const float \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+quant\+\_\+uvalue\+\_\+plane2}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the error of a decimated weight set for 2 planes. 

After computing ideal weights for the case with one weight per texel, we want to compute the error for decimated weight grids where weights are stored at a lower resolution. This function computes the error of the reduced grid, compared to the full grid.


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em eai1} & The ideal weights for the full grid and plane 1. \\
\hline
{\em eai2} & The ideal weights for the full grid and plane 2. \\
\hline
{\em di} & The selected weight decimation. \\
\hline
{\em dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+quant\+\_\+uvalue\+\_\+plane1} & The quantized weights for the decimated grid plane 1. \\
\hline
{\em dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+quant\+\_\+uvalue\+\_\+plane2} & The quantized weights for the decimated grid plane 2.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The accumulated error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_ac4a96475fb0074ef3fd0f08ea66de75e}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!compute\_error\_squared\_rgb@{compute\_error\_squared\_rgb}}
\index{compute\_error\_squared\_rgb@{compute\_error\_squared\_rgb}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{compute\_error\_squared\_rgb()}{compute\_error\_squared\_rgb()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_ac4a96475fb0074ef3fd0f08ea66de75e} 
void compute\+\_\+error\+\_\+squared\+\_\+rgb (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__info}{partition\+\_\+info}} \&}]{pi}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__lines3}{partition\+\_\+lines3}}}]{plines}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONS\mbox{]}, }\item[{float \&}]{uncor\+\_\+error}{, }\item[{float \&}]{samec\+\_\+error}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the RGB error for uncorrelated and same chroma projections. 

The output of compute averages and dirs is post processed to define two lines, both of which go through the mean-\/color-\/value. One line has a direction defined by the dominant direction; this is used to assess the error from using an uncorrelated color representation. The other line goes through (0,0,0) and is used to assess the error from using an RGBS color representation.

This function computes the squared error when using these two representations.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em pi} & The partition info for the current trial. \\
\hline
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to be compressed. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em plines} & Processed line inputs, and line length outputs. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em uncor\+\_\+error} & The cumulative error for using the uncorrelated line. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em samec\+\_\+error} & The cumulative error for using the same chroma line. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{compute\_error\_squared\_rgba()}{compute\_error\_squared\_rgba()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a2dec702033b002eaf4090eb47ce4ad21} 
void compute\+\_\+error\+\_\+squared\+\_\+rgba (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__info}{partition\+\_\+info}} \&}]{pi}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structprocessed__line4}{processed\+\_\+line4}}}]{uncor\+\_\+plines}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONS\mbox{]}, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structprocessed__line4}{processed\+\_\+line4}}}]{samec\+\_\+plines}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONS\mbox{]}, }\item[{float}]{line\+\_\+lengths}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONS\mbox{]}, }\item[{float \&}]{uncor\+\_\+error}{, }\item[{float \&}]{samec\+\_\+error}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the RGBA error for uncorrelated and same chroma projections. 

The output of compute averages and dirs is post processed to define two lines, both of which go through the mean-\/color-\/value. One line has a direction defined by the dominant direction; this is used to assess the error from using an uncorrelated color representation. The other line goes through (0,0,0,1) and is used to assess the error from using an RGBS color representation.

This function computes the squared error when using these two representations.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em pi} & The partition info for the current trial. \\
\hline
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to be compressed. \\
\hline
 & {\em uncor\+\_\+plines} & Processed uncorrelated partition lines for each partition. \\
\hline
 & {\em samec\+\_\+plines} & Processed same chroma partition lines for each partition. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em line\+\_\+lengths} & The length of each components deviation from the line. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em uncor\+\_\+error} & The cumulative error for using the uncorrelated line. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em samec\+\_\+error} & The cumulative error for using the same chroma line. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_afa8cab65d4b6f0cbece52eec38aed523}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!compute\_ideal\_colors\_and\_weights\_1plane@{compute\_ideal\_colors\_and\_weights\_1plane}}
\index{compute\_ideal\_colors\_and\_weights\_1plane@{compute\_ideal\_colors\_and\_weights\_1plane}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{compute\_ideal\_colors\_and\_weights\_1plane()}{compute\_ideal\_colors\_and\_weights\_1plane()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_afa8cab65d4b6f0cbece52eec38aed523} 
void compute\+\_\+ideal\+\_\+colors\+\_\+and\+\_\+weights\+\_\+1plane (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__info}{partition\+\_\+info}} \&}]{pi}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structendpoints__and__weights}{endpoints\+\_\+and\+\_\+weights}} \&}]{ei}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute ideal endpoint colors and weights for 1 plane of weights. 

The ideal endpoints define a color line for the partition. For each texel the ideal weight defines an exact position on the partition color line. We can then use these to assess the error introduced by removing and quantizing the weight grid.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to compress. \\
\hline
 & {\em pi} & The partition info for the current trial. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em ei} & The endpoint and weight values. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_a52d3985007cfc83025661e0347bc00cc}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!compute\_ideal\_colors\_and\_weights\_2planes@{compute\_ideal\_colors\_and\_weights\_2planes}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{compute\_ideal\_colors\_and\_weights\_2planes()}{compute\_ideal\_colors\_and\_weights\_2planes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a52d3985007cfc83025661e0347bc00cc} 
void compute\+\_\+ideal\+\_\+colors\+\_\+and\+\_\+weights\+\_\+2planes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{plane2\+\_\+component}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structendpoints__and__weights}{endpoints\+\_\+and\+\_\+weights}} \&}]{ei1}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structendpoints__and__weights}{endpoints\+\_\+and\+\_\+weights}} \&}]{ei2}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute ideal endpoint colors and weights for 2 planes of weights. 

The ideal endpoints define a color line for the partition. For each texel the ideal weight defines an exact position on the partition color line. We can then use these to assess the error introduced by removing and quantizing the weight grid.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em bsd} & The block size information. \\
\hline
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to compress. \\
\hline
 & {\em plane2\+\_\+component} & The component assigned to plane 2. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em ei1} & The endpoint and weight values for plane 1. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em ei2} & The endpoint and weight values for plane 2. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{compute\_ideal\_endpoint\_formats()}{compute\_ideal\_endpoint\_formats()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a81c7b68e8c7b82a5ff718f21bd4f3c35} 
unsigned int compute\+\_\+ideal\+\_\+endpoint\+\_\+formats (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__info}{partition\+\_\+info}} \&}]{pi}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structendpoints}{endpoints}} \&}]{ep}{, }\item[{const int8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{qwt\+\_\+bitcounts}{, }\item[{const float \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{qwt\+\_\+errors}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{tune\+\_\+candidate\+\_\+limit}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{start\+\_\+block\+\_\+mode}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{end\+\_\+block\+\_\+mode}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{partition\+\_\+format\+\_\+specifiers}{\mbox{[}\+TUNE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+TRIAL\+\_\+\+CANDIDATES\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONS\mbox{]}, }\item[{int}]{block\+\_\+mode}{\mbox{[}\+TUNE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+TRIAL\+\_\+\+CANDIDATES\mbox{]}, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_a806a5b8001942a6fa06d788ffec45a75}{quant\+\_\+method}}}]{quant\+\_\+level}{\mbox{[}\+TUNE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+TRIAL\+\_\+\+CANDIDATES\mbox{]}, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_a806a5b8001942a6fa06d788ffec45a75}{quant\+\_\+method}}}]{quant\+\_\+level\+\_\+mod}{\mbox{[}\+TUNE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+TRIAL\+\_\+\+CANDIDATES\mbox{]}, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structcompression__working__buffers}{compression\+\_\+working\+\_\+buffers}} \&}]{tmpbuf}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Identify, for each mode, which set of color endpoint produces the best result. 

Returns the best {\ttfamily tune\+\_\+candidate\+\_\+limit} best looking modes, along with the ideal color encoding combination for each. The modified quantization level can be used when all formats are the same, as this frees up two additional bits of storage.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em pi} & The partition info for the current trial. \\
\hline
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to compress. \\
\hline
 & {\em ep} & The ideal endpoints. \\
\hline
 & {\em qwt\+\_\+bitcounts} & Bit counts for different quantization methods. \\
\hline
 & {\em qwt\+\_\+errors} & Errors for different quantization methods. \\
\hline
 & {\em tune\+\_\+candidate\+\_\+limit} & The max number of candidates to return, may be less. \\
\hline
 & {\em start\+\_\+block\+\_\+mode} & The first block mode to inspect. \\
\hline
 & {\em end\+\_\+block\+\_\+mode} & The last block mode to inspect. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em partition\+\_\+format\+\_\+specifiers} & The best formats per partition. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em \doxylink{structblock__mode}{block\+\_\+mode}} & The best packed block mode indexes. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em quant\+\_\+level} & The best color quant level. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em quant\+\_\+level\+\_\+mod} & The best color quant level if endpoints are the same. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em tmpbuf} & Preallocated scratch buffers for the compressor.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The actual number of candidate matches returned. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

void compute\+\_\+ideal\+\_\+weights\+\_\+for\+\_\+decimation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structendpoints__and__weights}{endpoints\+\_\+and\+\_\+weights}} \&}]{ei}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structdecimation__info}{decimation\+\_\+info}} \&}]{di}{, }\item[{float \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+ideal\+\_\+value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the optimal unquantized weights for a decimation table. 

After computing ideal weights for the case for a complete weight grid, we we want to compute the ideal weights for the case where weights exist only for some texels. We do this with a steepest-\/descent grid solver which works as follows\+:

First, for each actual weight, perform a weighted averaging of the texels affected by the weight. Then, set step size to $<$some initial value$>$ and attempt one step towards the original ideal weight if it helps to reduce error.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em ei} & The non-\/decimated endpoints and weights. \\
\hline
 & {\em di} & The selected weight decimation. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+ideal\+\_\+value} & The ideal values for the decimated weight set. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{compute\_pixel\_region\_variance()}{compute\_pixel\_region\_variance()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a8cd8e456dcff495dba9b6666be024007} 
void compute\+\_\+pixel\+\_\+region\+\_\+variance (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__contexti}{astcenc\+\_\+contexti}} \&}]{ctx}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpixel__region__args}{pixel\+\_\+region\+\_\+args}} \&}]{arg}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute averages for a pixel region. 

The routine computes both in a single pass, using a summed-\/area table to decouple the running time from the averaging/variance kernel size.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em ctx} & The compressor context storing the output data. \\
\hline
 & {\em arg} & The input parameter structure. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{compute\_quantized\_weights\_for\_decimation()}{compute\_quantized\_weights\_for\_decimation()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_ac7f0846913e68db929ae621f56c209ce} 
void compute\+\_\+quantized\+\_\+weights\+\_\+for\+\_\+decimation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structdecimation__info}{decimation\+\_\+info}} \&}]{di}{, }\item[{float}]{low\+\_\+bound}{, }\item[{float}]{high\+\_\+bound}{, }\item[{const float \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+ideal\+\_\+value}{, }\item[{float \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+quant\+\_\+uvalue}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+uquant}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_a806a5b8001942a6fa06d788ffec45a75}{quant\+\_\+method}}}]{quant\+\_\+level}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the optimal quantized weights for a decimation table. 

We test the two closest weight indices in the allowed quantization range and keep the weight that is the closest match.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em di} & The selected weight decimation. \\
\hline
 & {\em low\+\_\+bound} & The lowest weight allowed. \\
\hline
 & {\em high\+\_\+bound} & The highest weight allowed. \\
\hline
 & {\em dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+ideal\+\_\+value} & The ideal weight set. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+quant\+\_\+uvalue} & The output quantized weight as a float. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em dec\+\_\+weight\+\_\+uquant} & The output quantized weight as encoded int. \\
\hline
 & {\em quant\+\_\+level} & The desired weight quant level. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

float compute\+\_\+symbolic\+\_\+block\+\_\+difference\+\_\+1plane (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__config}{astcenc\+\_\+config}} \&}]{config}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsymbolic__compressed__block}{symbolic\+\_\+compressed\+\_\+block}} \&}]{scb}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the error between a symbolic block and the original input data. 

This function is specialized for 1 plane and N partition search.

In RGBM mode this will reject blocks that attempt to encode a zero M value.


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em config} & The compressor config. \\
\hline
{\em bsd} & The block size information. \\
\hline
{\em scb} & The symbolic compressed encoding. \\
\hline
{\em blk} & The original image block color data.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
Returns the computed error, or a negative value if the encoding should be rejected for any reason. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

float compute\+\_\+symbolic\+\_\+block\+\_\+difference\+\_\+1plane\+\_\+1partition (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__config}{astcenc\+\_\+config}} \&}]{config}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsymbolic__compressed__block}{symbolic\+\_\+compressed\+\_\+block}} \&}]{scb}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the error between a symbolic block and the original input data. 

This function is specialized for 1 plane and 1 partition search.

In RGBM mode this will reject blocks that attempt to encode a zero M value.


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em config} & The compressor config. \\
\hline
{\em bsd} & The block size information. \\
\hline
{\em scb} & The symbolic compressed encoding. \\
\hline
{\em blk} & The original image block color data.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
Returns the computed error, or a negative value if the encoding should be rejected for any reason. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_a9c23f8373c9f5e708650b7c8e038b182}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!compute\_symbolic\_block\_difference\_2plane@{compute\_symbolic\_block\_difference\_2plane}}
\index{compute\_symbolic\_block\_difference\_2plane@{compute\_symbolic\_block\_difference\_2plane}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{compute\_symbolic\_block\_difference\_2plane()}{compute\_symbolic\_block\_difference\_2plane()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a9c23f8373c9f5e708650b7c8e038b182} 
float compute\+\_\+symbolic\+\_\+block\+\_\+difference\+\_\+2plane (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__config}{astcenc\+\_\+config}} \&}]{config}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsymbolic__compressed__block}{symbolic\+\_\+compressed\+\_\+block}} \&}]{scb}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the error between a symbolic block and the original input data. 

This function is specialized for 2 plane and 1 partition search.

In RGBM mode this will reject blocks that attempt to encode a zero M value.


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em config} & The compressor config. \\
\hline
{\em bsd} & The block size information. \\
\hline
{\em scb} & The symbolic compressed encoding. \\
\hline
{\em blk} & The original image block color data.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
Returns the computed error, or a negative value if the encoding should be rejected for any reason. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{decode\_ise()}{decode\_ise()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a1cc25f0a98b60ff2bc5fd65f6b4190fa} 
void decode\+\_\+ise (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_a806a5b8001942a6fa06d788ffec45a75}{quant\+\_\+method}}}]{quant\+\_\+level}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{character\+\_\+count}{, }\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{input\+\_\+data}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{output\+\_\+data}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{bit\+\_\+offset}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Decode a packed string using BISE. 

Note that BISE input strings are not a whole number of bytes in length, and ASTC can start strings at arbitrary bit offsets in the encoded data.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em quant\+\_\+level} & The BISE alphabet size. \\
\hline
 & {\em character\+\_\+count} & The number of characters in the string. \\
\hline
 & {\em input\+\_\+data} & The packed string. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em output\+\_\+data} & The output storage, one byte per character. \\
\hline
 & {\em bit\+\_\+offset} & The starting offset in the output storage. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a4a5f09c362972951a31e4d7ff918f89f} 
void decompress\+\_\+symbolic\+\_\+block (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc_8h_adf71df2e9f79916ccc02886ba1bdeb29}{astcenc\+\_\+profile}}}]{decode\+\_\+mode}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{int}]{xpos}{, }\item[{int}]{ypos}{, }\item[{int}]{zpos}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsymbolic__compressed__block}{symbolic\+\_\+compressed\+\_\+block}} \&}]{scb}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Decompress a symbolic block in to an image block. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em decode\+\_\+mode} & The decode mode (LDR, HDR, etc). \\
\hline
 & {\em bsd} & The block size information. \\
\hline
 & {\em xpos} & The X coordinate of the block in the overall image. \\
\hline
 & {\em ypos} & The Y coordinate of the block in the overall image. \\
\hline
 & {\em zpos} & The Z coordinate of the block in the overall image. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em blk} & The decompressed image block color data. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{encode\_ise@{encode\_ise}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{encode\_ise()}{encode\_ise()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a1e3b68510a3fa2766d2decf242132f2f} 
void encode\+\_\+ise (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_a806a5b8001942a6fa06d788ffec45a75}{quant\+\_\+method}}}]{quant\+\_\+level}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{character\+\_\+count}{, }\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{input\+\_\+data}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{output\+\_\+data}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{bit\+\_\+offset}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Encode a packed string using BISE. 

Note that BISE can return strings that are not a whole number of bytes in length, and ASTC can start storing strings in a block at arbitrary bit offsets in the encoded data.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em quant\+\_\+level} & The BISE alphabet size. \\
\hline
 & {\em character\+\_\+count} & The number of characters in the string. \\
\hline
 & {\em input\+\_\+data} & The unpacked string, one byte per character. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em output\+\_\+data} & The output packed string. \\
\hline
 & {\em bit\+\_\+offset} & The starting offset in the output storage. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_a7577b3047a3f9f0fe44fd579f5450630}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!find\_best\_partition\_candidates@{find\_best\_partition\_candidates}}
\index{find\_best\_partition\_candidates@{find\_best\_partition\_candidates}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{find\_best\_partition\_candidates()}{find\_best\_partition\_candidates()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a7577b3047a3f9f0fe44fd579f5450630} 
unsigned int find\+\_\+best\+\_\+partition\+\_\+candidates (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{partition\+\_\+count}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{partition\+\_\+search\+\_\+limit}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{best\+\_\+partitions}{\mbox{[}\+TUNE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONING\+\_\+\+CANDIDATES\mbox{]}, }\item[{unsigned int}]{requested\+\_\+candidates}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Find the best set of partitions to trial for a given block. 

On return the {\ttfamily best\+\_\+partitions} list will contain the two best partition candidates; one assuming data has uncorrelated chroma and one assuming the data has correlated chroma. The best candidate is returned first in the list.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em bsd} & The block size information. \\
\hline
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to compress. \\
\hline
 & {\em partition\+\_\+count} & The number of partitions in the block. \\
\hline
 & {\em partition\+\_\+search\+\_\+limit} & The number of candidate partition encodings to trial. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em best\+\_\+partitions} & The best partition candidates. \\
\hline
 & {\em requested\+\_\+candidates} & The number of requested partitionings. May return fewer if candidates are not available.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The actual number of candidates returned. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_2d\_percentile\_table()}{get\_2d\_percentile\_table()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_af98304be147ac93a80eaf13cbe448605} 
const float \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} get\+\_\+2d\+\_\+percentile\+\_\+table (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned int}]{xdim}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{ydim}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the percentile table for 2D block modes. 

This is an empirically determined prioritization of which block modes to use in the search in terms of their centile (lower centiles = more useful).

Returns a dynamically allocated array; caller must free with delete\mbox{[}\mbox{]}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em xdim} & The block x size. \\
\hline
{\em ydim} & The block y size.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The unpacked table. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_af46c9322b401332698e9cb93c968fe19}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!get\_ise\_sequence\_bitcount@{get\_ise\_sequence\_bitcount}}
\index{get\_ise\_sequence\_bitcount@{get\_ise\_sequence\_bitcount}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_ise\_sequence\_bitcount()}{get\_ise\_sequence\_bitcount()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_af46c9322b401332698e9cb93c968fe19} 
unsigned int get\+\_\+ise\+\_\+sequence\+\_\+bitcount (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned int}]{character\+\_\+count}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_a806a5b8001942a6fa06d788ffec45a75}{quant\+\_\+method}}}]{quant\+\_\+level}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return the number of bits needed to encode an ISE sequence. 

This implementation assumes that the {\ttfamily quant} level is untrusted, given it may come from random data being decompressed, so we return an arbitrary unencodable size if that is the case.


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em character\+\_\+count} & The number of items in the sequence. \\
\hline
{\em quant\+\_\+level} & The desired quantization level.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The number of bits needed to encode the BISE string. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Populate the block size descriptor for the target block size. 

This will also initialize the partition table metadata, which is stored as part of the BSD structure.

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_a3f9cb247b3a6133147c430dfd81b3d96}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!init\_compute\_averages@{init\_compute\_averages}}
\index{init\_compute\_averages@{init\_compute\_averages}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{init\_compute\_averages()}{init\_compute\_averages()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a3f9cb247b3a6133147c430dfd81b3d96} 
unsigned int init\+\_\+compute\+\_\+averages (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \&}]{img}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{alpha\+\_\+kernel\+\_\+radius}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__swizzle}{astcenc\+\_\+swizzle}} \&}]{swz}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structavg__args}{avg\+\_\+args}} \&}]{ag}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Setup computation of regional averages in an image. 

This must be done by only a single thread per image, before any thread calls {\ttfamily \doxylink{astcenc__entry_8cpp_abb4b489d57171cfb1ebe0be7d24ef1d9}{compute\+\_\+averages()}}.

Results are written back into {\ttfamily img-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}input\+\_\+alpha\+\_\+averages}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em img} & The input image data, also holds output data. \\
\hline
 & {\em alpha\+\_\+kernel\+\_\+radius} & The kernel radius (in pixels) for alpha mods. \\
\hline
 & {\em swz} & Input data component swizzle. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em ag} & The average variance arguments to init.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The number of tasks in the processing stage. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a9460ca3acf0175a93580b78d5d99a36a} 
void init\+\_\+partition\+\_\+tables (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{bool}]{can\+\_\+omit\+\_\+partitionings}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{partition\+\_\+count\+\_\+cutoff}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Populate the partition tables for the target block size. 

Note the {\ttfamily bsd} descriptor must be initialized by calling {\ttfamily \doxylink{astcenc__internal_8h_a5c46863585cc583c3deb49323dfb73d8}{init\+\_\+block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor()}} before calling this function.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em bsd} & The block size information structure to populate. \\
\hline
 & {\em can\+\_\+omit\+\_\+partitionings} & True if we can we drop partitionings that astcenc won\textquotesingle{}t use. \\
\hline
 & {\em partition\+\_\+count\+\_\+cutoff} & The partition count cutoff to use, if we can omit partitionings. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a04e3f01eb10a8a494e1d07b39c496bde} 
void load\+\_\+image\+\_\+block\+\_\+fast\+\_\+ldr (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc_8h_adf71df2e9f79916ccc02886ba1bdeb29}{astcenc\+\_\+profile}}}]{decode\+\_\+mode}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__image}{astcenc\+\_\+image}} \&}]{img}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{xpos}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{ypos}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{zpos}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structastcenc__swizzle}{astcenc\+\_\+swizzle}} \&}]{swz}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Load a single image block from the input image. 

This specialized variant can be used only if the block is 2D LDR U8 data, with no swizzle.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em decode\+\_\+mode} & The compression color profile. \\
\hline
 & {\em img} & The input image data. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em blk} & The image block to populate. \\
\hline
 & {\em bsd} & The block size information. \\
\hline
 & {\em xpos} & The block X coordinate in the input image. \\
\hline
 & {\em ypos} & The block Y coordinate in the input image. \\
\hline
 & {\em zpos} & The block Z coordinate in the input image. \\
\hline
 & {\em swz} & The swizzle to apply on load. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pack\_color\_endpoints()}{pack\_color\_endpoints()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_ab9f9b564c57688af1f8fc1d9e000af81} 
uint8\+\_\+t pack\+\_\+color\+\_\+endpoints (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvfloat4}{vfloat4}}}]{color0}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvfloat4}{vfloat4}}}]{color1}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvfloat4}{vfloat4}}}]{rgbs\+\_\+color}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvfloat4}{vfloat4}}}]{rgbo\+\_\+color}{, }\item[{int}]{format}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{output}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_a806a5b8001942a6fa06d788ffec45a75}{quant\+\_\+method}}}]{quant\+\_\+level}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Pack a single pair of color endpoints as effectively as possible. 

The user requests a base color endpoint mode in {\ttfamily format}, but the quantizer may choose a delta-\/based representation. It will report back the format variant it actually used.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em color0} & The input unquantized color0 endpoint for absolute endpoint pairs. \\
\hline
 & {\em color1} & The input unquantized color1 endpoint for absolute endpoint pairs. \\
\hline
 & {\em rgbs\+\_\+color} & The input unquantized RGBS variant endpoint for same chroma endpoints. \\
\hline
 & {\em rgbo\+\_\+color} & The input unquantized RGBS variant endpoint for HDR endpoints. \\
\hline
 & {\em format} & The desired base format. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em output} & The output storage for the quantized colors/ \\
\hline
 & {\em quant\+\_\+level} & The quantization level requested.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
The actual endpoint mode used. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_acd6272d8cee006f73e936e16739c4cab}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!physical\_to\_symbolic@{physical\_to\_symbolic}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{physical\_to\_symbolic()}{physical\_to\_symbolic()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_acd6272d8cee006f73e936e16739c4cab} 
void physical\+\_\+to\+\_\+symbolic (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t}]{pcb}{\mbox{[}16\mbox{]}, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structsymbolic__compressed__block}{symbolic\+\_\+compressed\+\_\+block}} \&}]{scb}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Convert a binary physical encoding into a symbolic representation. 

This function can cope with arbitrary input data; output blocks will be flagged as an error block if the encoding is invalid.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em bsd} & The block size information. \\
\hline
 & {\em pcb} & The physical compresesd block input. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em scb} & The output symbolic representation. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_a02bcad94240678ee727ccf2f0fbfb5d3}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!recompute\_ideal\_colors\_1plane@{recompute\_ideal\_colors\_1plane}}
\index{recompute\_ideal\_colors\_1plane@{recompute\_ideal\_colors\_1plane}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{recompute\_ideal\_colors\_1plane()}{recompute\_ideal\_colors\_1plane()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a02bcad94240678ee727ccf2f0fbfb5d3} 
void recompute\+\_\+ideal\+\_\+colors\+\_\+1plane (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpartition__info}{partition\+\_\+info}} \&}]{pi}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structdecimation__info}{decimation\+\_\+info}} \&}]{di}{, }\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dec\+\_\+weights\+\_\+uquant}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structendpoints}{endpoints}} \&}]{ep}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvfloat4}{vfloat4}}}]{rgbs\+\_\+vectors}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONS\mbox{]}, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvfloat4}{vfloat4}}}]{rgbo\+\_\+vectors}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+PARTITIONS\mbox{]}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



For a given 1 plane weight set recompute the endpoint colors. 

As we quantize and decimate weights the optimal endpoint colors may change slightly, so we must recompute the ideal colors for a specific weight set.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to compress. \\
\hline
 & {\em pi} & The partition info for the current trial. \\
\hline
 & {\em di} & The weight grid decimation table. \\
\hline
 & {\em dec\+\_\+weights\+\_\+uquant} & The quantized weight set. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em ep} & The color endpoints (modifed in place). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em rgbs\+\_\+vectors} & The RGB+scale vectors for LDR blocks. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em rgbo\+\_\+vectors} & The RGB+offset vectors for HDR blocks. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{recompute\_ideal\_colors\_2planes()}{recompute\_ideal\_colors\_2planes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_afb3c455470bef24f48d7815bb78bb569} 
void recompute\+\_\+ideal\+\_\+colors\+\_\+2planes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structimage__block}{image\+\_\+block}} \&}]{blk}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structdecimation__info}{decimation\+\_\+info}} \&}]{di}{, }\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dec\+\_\+weights\+\_\+uquant\+\_\+plane1}{, }\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dec\+\_\+weights\+\_\+uquant\+\_\+plane2}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structendpoints}{endpoints}} \&}]{ep}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvfloat4}{vfloat4}} \&}]{rgbs\+\_\+vector}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvfloat4}{vfloat4}} \&}]{rgbo\+\_\+vector}{, }\item[{int}]{plane2\+\_\+component}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



For a given 2 plane weight set recompute the endpoint colors. 

As we quantize and decimate weights the optimal endpoint colors may change slightly, so we must recompute the ideal colors for a specific weight set.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em blk} & The image block color data to compress. \\
\hline
 & {\em bsd} & The block\+\_\+size descriptor. \\
\hline
 & {\em di} & The weight grid decimation table. \\
\hline
 & {\em dec\+\_\+weights\+\_\+uquant\+\_\+plane1} & The quantized weight set for plane 1. \\
\hline
 & {\em dec\+\_\+weights\+\_\+uquant\+\_\+plane2} & The quantized weight set for plane 2. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em ep} & The color endpoints (modifed in place). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em rgbs\+\_\+vector} & The RGB+scale color for LDR blocks. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em rgbo\+\_\+vector} & The RGB+offset color for HDR blocks. \\
\hline
 & {\em plane2\+\_\+component} & The component assigned to plane 2. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_af7b1f1696c0ee5cbfd6f2546fa400011}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!symbolic\_to\_physical@{symbolic\_to\_physical}}
\index{symbolic\_to\_physical@{symbolic\_to\_physical}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{symbolic\_to\_physical()}{symbolic\_to\_physical()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_af7b1f1696c0ee5cbfd6f2546fa400011} 
void symbolic\+\_\+to\+\_\+physical (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsymbolic__compressed__block}{symbolic\+\_\+compressed\+\_\+block}} \&}]{scb}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{pcb}{\mbox{[}16\mbox{]}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Convert a symbolic representation into a binary physical encoding. 

It is assumed that the symbolic encoding is valid and encodable, or previously flagged as an error block if an error color it to be encoded.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em bsd} & The block size information. \\
\hline
 & {\em scb} & The symbolic representation. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em pcb} & The physical compressed block output. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_ab9b659180fb522b05391892336dbc095}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!unpack\_color\_endpoints@{unpack\_color\_endpoints}}
\index{unpack\_color\_endpoints@{unpack\_color\_endpoints}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpack\_color\_endpoints()}{unpack\_color\_endpoints()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_ab9b659180fb522b05391892336dbc095} 
void unpack\+\_\+color\+\_\+endpoints (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc_8h_adf71df2e9f79916ccc02886ba1bdeb29}{astcenc\+\_\+profile}}}]{decode\+\_\+mode}{, }\item[{int}]{format}{, }\item[{const uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{input}{, }\item[{bool \&}]{rgb\+\_\+hdr}{, }\item[{bool \&}]{alpha\+\_\+hdr}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvint4}{vint4}} \&}]{output0}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structvint4}{vint4}} \&}]{output1}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Unpack a single pair of encoded endpoints. 

Endpoints must be unscrambled and converted into the 0-\/255 range before calling this functions.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em decode\+\_\+mode} & The decode mode (LDR, HDR, etc). \\
\hline
 & {\em format} & The color endpoint mode used. \\
\hline
 & {\em input} & The raw array of encoded input integers. The length of this array depends on {\ttfamily format}; it can be safely assumed to be large enough. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em rgb\+\_\+hdr} & Is the endpoint using HDR for the RGB channels? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em alpha\+\_\+hdr} & Is the endpoint using HDR for the A channel? \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em output0} & The output color for endpoint 0. \\
\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_aec197676ba4b10bf63a6523a775530d8} 
void unpack\+\_\+weights (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structblock__size__descriptor}{block\+\_\+size\+\_\+descriptor}} \&}]{bsd}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structsymbolic__compressed__block}{symbolic\+\_\+compressed\+\_\+block}} \&}]{scb}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structdecimation__info}{decimation\+\_\+info}} \&}]{di}{, }\item[{bool}]{is\+\_\+dual\+\_\+plane}{, }\item[{int}]{weights\+\_\+plane1}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+TEXELS\mbox{]}, }\item[{int}]{weights\+\_\+plane2}{\mbox{[}\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+TEXELS\mbox{]}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Unpack a set of quantized and decimated weights. 

TODO\+: Can we skip this for non-\/decimated weights now that the {\ttfamily scb} is already storing unquantized weights?


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{매개변수}
 & {\em bsd} & The block size information. \\
\hline
 & {\em scb} & The symbolic compressed encoding. \\
\hline
 & {\em di} & The weight grid decimation table. \\
\hline
 & {\em is\+\_\+dual\+\_\+plane} & {\ttfamily true} if this is a dual plane block, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em weights\+\_\+plane1} & The output array for storing the plane 1 weights. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em weights\+\_\+plane2} & The output array for storing the plane 2 weights. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

The precomputed table for unpacking color values.

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_afa0c1b0c21a8a2f803fe662cefa3f21a}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!color\_unquant\_to\_uquant\_tables@{color\_unquant\_to\_uquant\_tables}}
\index{color\_unquant\_to\_uquant\_tables@{color\_unquant\_to\_uquant\_tables}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{color\_unquant\_to\_uquant\_tables}{color\_unquant\_to\_uquant\_tables}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_afa0c1b0c21a8a2f803fe662cefa3f21a} 
const uint8\+\_\+t color\+\_\+unquant\+\_\+to\+\_\+uquant\+\_\+tables\mbox{[}17\mbox{]}\mbox{[}512\mbox{]}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



The precomputed table for quantizing color values. 

Converts unquant value in 0-\/255 range into quant value in 0-\/255 range. No BISE scrambling is applied at this stage.

The BISE encoding results in ties where available quant$<$256$>$ values are equidistant the available quant$<$\+BISE$>$ values. This table stores two values for each input -\/ one for use with a negative residual, and one for use with a positive residual.

Indexed by \mbox{[}quant\+\_\+mode -\/ 4\mbox{]}\mbox{[}data\+\_\+value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 2 + residual\mbox{]}.

The precomputed table for quantizing color values. 

\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_source}{astcenc\+\_\+quantization.\+cpp}} 파일의 \mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_source_l00027}{27}} 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_a834f3531350f3a55d6271b4dc18a223d}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!color\_uquant\_to\_scrambled\_pquant\_tables@{color\_uquant\_to\_scrambled\_pquant\_tables}}
\index{color\_uquant\_to\_scrambled\_pquant\_tables@{color\_uquant\_to\_scrambled\_pquant\_tables}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{color\_uquant\_to\_scrambled\_pquant\_tables}{color\_uquant\_to\_scrambled\_pquant\_tables}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a834f3531350f3a55d6271b4dc18a223d} 
const uint8\+\_\+t color\+\_\+uquant\+\_\+to\+\_\+scrambled\+\_\+pquant\+\_\+tables\mbox{[}17\mbox{]}\mbox{[}256\mbox{]}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



The precomputed table for packing quantized color values. 

Converts quant value in 0-\/255 range into packed quant value in 0-\/N range, with BISE scrambling applied.

Indexed by \mbox{[}quant\+\_\+mode -\/ 4\mbox{]}\mbox{[}data\+\_\+value\mbox{]}. 

\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_source}{astcenc\+\_\+quantization.\+cpp}} 파일의 \mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_source_l00338}{338}} 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

\index{quant\_mode\_table@{quant\_mode\_table}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{quant\_mode\_table}{quant\_mode\_table}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_a67050b7e3e5e5c4ff2021c8f266dd903} 
const int8\+\_\+t quant\+\_\+mode\+\_\+table\mbox{[}10\mbox{]}\mbox{[}128\mbox{]}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



The precomputed quant mode storage table. 

Indexing by \mbox{[}integer\+\_\+count/2\mbox{]}\mbox{[}bits\mbox{]} gives us the quantization level for a given integer count and number of compressed storage bits. Returns -\/1 for cases where the requested integer count cannot ever fit in the supplied storage size. 

\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_source}{astcenc\+\_\+quantization.\+cpp}} 파일의 \mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_source_l00802}{802}} 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

\Hypertarget{astcenc__internal_8h_ab2ec26aaf33ca112e7c7d098ef3e7dc9}\index{astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}!TUNE\_MAX\_ANGULAR\_QUANT@{TUNE\_MAX\_ANGULAR\_QUANT}}
\index{TUNE\_MAX\_ANGULAR\_QUANT@{TUNE\_MAX\_ANGULAR\_QUANT}!astcenc\_internal.h@{astcenc\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{TUNE\_MAX\_ANGULAR\_QUANT}{TUNE\_MAX\_ANGULAR\_QUANT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__internal_8h_ab2ec26aaf33ca112e7c7d098ef3e7dc9} 
unsigned int TUNE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+ANGULAR\+\_\+\+QUANT \{ 7 \}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}, {\ttfamily [constexpr]}}



The maximum quant level using full angular endpoint search method. 

The angular endpoint search is used to find the min/max weight that should be used for a given quantization level. It is effective but expensive, so we only use it where it has the most value -\/ low quant levels with wide spacing. It is used below TUNE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+ANGULAR\+\_\+\+QUANT (inclusive). Above this we assume the min weight is 0.\+0f, and the max weight is 1.\+0f.

Note the angular algorithm is vectorized, and using QUANT\+\_\+12 exactly fills one 8-\/wide vector. Decreasing by one doesn\textquotesingle{}t buy much performance, and increasing by one is disproportionately expensive. 

\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_source}{astcenc\+\_\+internal.\+h}} 파일의 \mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__internal_8h_source_l00154}{154}} 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00154\ \{\ 7\ \};\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ QUANT\_12\ */}}

\end{DoxyCode}
